[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[39mat [0m[1;35mExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[39mExpanderFuzzer.jav[0m[1;92ma:52[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDEDUP_TOKEN: a87e9aa6b0374484[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== libFuzzer crashing input ==[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA critical security issue was detected during fuzz testing of the Apache Commons [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompress `Expander` example. The Jazzer sanitizer flagged a file path traversal [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability when expanding archive entries whose paths include “..” segments. The[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue surfaced as a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: File path traversal` exception, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating that extraction logic can be manipulated to write files outside the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintended output directory.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzzing, an archive file containing a crafted entry path [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`q/r/s/t/..[0m[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was passed to the `Expander.expand` method. The [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minternal sanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FilePathTraversal.check`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detected that resolving the entry’s [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelative path would escape the designated output root, triggering a security [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexception.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  File path traversal: attackers can craft archive entry names with `..` segments [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto cause files to be written outside of the intended extraction directory.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations and findings  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates from [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.FilePathTraversal.pathFirstArgHook`, which[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintercepts calls processing the archive entry paths.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Stack trace illustrates repeated invocations of `Expander.expand` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mat lines [0m[1;36m86[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m204[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m324[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m400[0m[39m, and [0m[1;36m460[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating recursive or multi-stage expansion logic.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m serves solely to drive[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs into the `Expander` code and is not the root cause.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The problematic path in the crash report [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/tmp/.../output/q/r/s/t/../../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates traversal through [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple directory levels.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate for a holistic view  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `[0m[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream, File[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and its overloads in [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially at the line [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnumbers shown in the trace[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Path normalization and resolution logic within `Expander` that constructs [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget file paths for extracted entries.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Any internal or third-party utilities used by `Expander` to create directories[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor write files [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `FileOutputStream`, `Files.create*`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The `FilePathTraversal` sanitizer implementation in Jazzer [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`FilePathTraversal.check`, `checkPath`, `pathFirstArgHook`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to understand exactly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich checks are applied and where they hook into the code.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential interactions between path resolution and archive entry metadata [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39me.g., absolute vs. relative paths, symbolic links[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo root-cause analysis or remediation steps are provided here; this report focuses [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msolely on summarizing the observed path traversal detection and identifying the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrelevant code areas for further investigation.[0m                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m86[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:            return outputFile;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue Summary & Root Cause  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability stems from `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returning a [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mURL‐decoded `Path` without normalization. Although the method initially checks a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalized `outputFile` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mraw name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m against zip‐slip via `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit then returns  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mname, [0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     without calling `[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. An attacker can craft an entry name [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining `%2e%2e` segments[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that decodes to `..` and thus escape the intended [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput directory at write time.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Critical Logic to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - URL‐decoding of entry names to support encoded entry names.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Zip‐slip guard: rejecting decoded names that would escape the target [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectory.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Backward compatibility: if decoding fails, falling back to the raw entry name.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Strategy  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Refactor `[0m[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` so that decoding happens [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore resolving and normalization, and both the zip‐slip check and return value [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muse the decoded+normalized path. Specifically:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Decode `[0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in a try/catch; fallback to the raw name on exception.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Resolve the decoded name against `parentPath` and immediately call [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Perform the `[0m[1;35mstartsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` guard on the decoded+normalized [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Path`.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Return the decoded+normalized `Path`.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Remove the legacy two‐step approach [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnormalize first on raw name then return [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man unnormalized decode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Consolidate to a single [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecode→resolve→normalize→check→return flow.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. No other parts of the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding `Expander`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m require modification, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msince they invoke `resolveIn` to obtain the safe extraction path.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Open `src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.java`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Replace the existing `resolveIn` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines ~[0m[1;36m78[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m90[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with the following [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfinal Path parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final String rawName = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          final String decodedName;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          try [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrawName, [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mIllegalArgumentException | UnsupportedEncodingException e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m If decoding fails, use the raw name[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              decodedName = rawName;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Resolve and normalize in one step[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Guard against zip‐slip: ensure the normalized path is within [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparentPath[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                  [0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, parentPath, decodedName, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutputFile[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return outputFile;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Remove any code branches that perform an initial normalization on the raw [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname followed by a second unnormalized resolve of the decoded name.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Rebuild and run existing unit tests and the `ExpanderFuzzer` harness to [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirm no regressions and that the path‐traversal issue is resolved.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification & Side‐Effects  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By decoding first and then normalizing, any `..` segments introduced by URL [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecoding are collapsed before the zip‐slip check and cannot escape the [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`parentPath`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The zip‐slip guard is applied exactly once on the same normalized path that is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturned, eliminating the discrepancy.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Existing functionality for URL‐encoded entry names is preserved; decoding [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfailures still fall back gracefully.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to harness code, fuzzing logic, or external [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibraries—compliance with patch guidelines.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Potential side effect: entry names that decode to extremely long or weird [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpaths will now be rejected if they attempt to escape, which is desirable for [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity. Normal valid entries remain unaffected.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Reference Code Ranges  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   <code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.jav[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92ma:78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         An AddressSanitizer-enabled fuzz run using Jazzer triggered a FilePathTraversal     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         security alert [1m([0m“zip slip”[1m)[0m in the example `Expander` code when expanding archive   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entries whose names contain “..” segments. To harden the path resolution, a patch   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         was proposed in the `[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath[1m)[0m` default method: it decodes the   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         entry name via `URLDecoder`, normalizes the target path, and enforces a parent-path [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         check before returning the resolved `Path`. After applying the patch, the Maven     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         build fails with a compilation error in `ArchiveEntry.java`—a definite-assignment   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         issue for the local variable `decodedName`.                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Initial Issue                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - During a Jazzer fuzzing session, a critical security sanitizer                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`FilePathTraversal.check`[1m)[0m detected a file-path-traversal [1m([0mzip-slip[1m)[0m scenario.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The stack trace shows the violation occurring in `[1;35mExpander.expand[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` [1m([0mmultiple [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         overloads[1m)[0m and ultimately in `[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` [1m([0mthe default method      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         introduced in version [1;36m1.26[0m.[1;36m0[0m[1m)[0m.                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The fuzzer input exploited a path like `q/r/s/t/..[35m/../[0m[95mjazzer-traversal[0m`, causing  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `[1;35mnormalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` to back up outside the intended output directory.                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Patch Attempt                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The patch modifies `[1;35mArchiveEntry.resolveIn[0m[1m([0mPath parentPath[1m)[0m`:                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. Rename `[1;35mgetName[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` result to `rawName`.                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. Introduce a local `final String decodedName;`                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. Wrap `[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1m([0mrawName, US_ASCII[1m)[0m` in a try/catch, assigning the      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         decoded or fallback value to `decodedName`.                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. Call `[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1m([0mdecodedName[1m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`, then check that the        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         resulting path starts with `parentPath`.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m5[0m. Throw an informative `IOException` on failure, referencing `decodedName`       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         instead of the raw name.                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m6[0m. Simplify the return path to only `outputFile`.                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The patch removes the second decoding attempt that was originally under the       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         try/catch at the end of the method.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Build Result After Patch                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Maven recompilation of `commons-compress` fails with:                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1m[[0mERROR[1m][0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/src/commons-compress/src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/[0m[95mArchiveEn[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [95mtry.java[0m:[1m[[0m[1;36m84[0m,[1;36m13[0m[1m][0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  variable decodedName might already have been assigned                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           ```                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - This indicates a Java definite-assignment analysis error: the compiler believes   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `decodedName` could be uninitialized or multiply initialized along some control     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         path.                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Areas for Further Investigation                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The default `resolveIn` implementation in `ArchiveEntry` [1m([0minterface[1m)[0m – verify     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         variable scoping, try/catch coverage, and definite-assignment rules.                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - All callers of `resolveIn` in `Expander` and other archive-expansion utilities,   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         to confirm consistent behavior and exception handling.                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Related APIs in other archive formats [1m([0me.g., tar, 7z[1m)[0m to ensure they apply the    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         same normalization and parent-directory checks.                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Any existing utility methods for safe path resolution within the codebase to      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         avoid duplicating logic.                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msrc/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/archivers/ArchiveEntry.jav[0m[1;92ma:78[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m82[0m[39m:            throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mString.format[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip '%s' + '%s' -> '%s'"[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mStandardCharsets.US_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m87[0m[39m:            return outputFile;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m88[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m89[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m90[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root cause analysis and core insight  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The compilation error “variable decodedName might already have been assigned” [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstems from declaring `decodedName` as `final` and then assigning it in both the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`try` block and the `catch` block. Although Java’s definite‐assignment rules allow [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmutually exclusive assignments in try/catch, the compiler in this context rejects [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple assignment sites for a final local variable.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Security‐wise, the original code normalized *before* decoding and [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munconditionally returned a second decode result without a corresponding post‐decode[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormalization or safety check, leaving a zip‐slip gap.  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve existing logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep the same API signature `default Path [0m[1;35mresolveIn[0m[1;39m([0m[39mPath parentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException`.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Retain the check that the resolved path must start with `parentPath`.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Avoid changes to callers [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Expander`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m or test harness code.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch outline  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Simplify `decodedName` handling to eliminate the definite‐assignment error:  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Declare and initialize `decodedName` in one statement [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`String decodedName [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m= rawName;`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In a `try` block, attempt to decode into `decodedName`; on any exception, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msilently retain the original.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - No `final` modifier on `decodedName`.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Perform *decode → normalize → safety check → return* in that exact order:  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `String rawName = [0m[1;35mgetName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `String decodedName = rawName;`  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         try `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m decodedName = [0m[1;35mURLDecoder.decode[0m[1;39m([0m[39mrawName, [0m[1;35mUS_ASCII.name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         catch any decoding exception `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[35m/[0m[39m* fallback to rawName *[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. `Path outputFile = [0m[1;35mparentPath.resolve[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdecodedName[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.normalize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. If `![0m[1;35moutputFile.startsWith[0m[1;39m([0m[39mparentPath[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, throw `[0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Zip slip [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m..."[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` using `decodedName` in the message.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. `return outputFile;`  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Step-by-step implementation instructions  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `ArchiveEntry.java`, replace the entire existing `resolveIn` default method[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbody with the improved sequence above.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove any `final String decodedName;` declaration and associated multi‐catch [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39massignments.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Import `java.net.URLDecoder` and `java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets` if not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malready.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure the method compiles under Java [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m+ and passes all existing unit and fuzz[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests unmodified.  [0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification and side‐effect mitigation  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This patch preserves the API and existing callers while resolving the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefinite‐assignment compilation error.  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It hardens the zip‐slip prevention by decoding first and then normalizing the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecoded name, ensuring no “..” segments survive untested.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By initializing `decodedName` to `rawName`, there is no uninitialized‐variable[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrisk. Removing the `final` modifier avoids multiple‐assignment conflicts.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Any legitimate archive entries containing percent‐encoded characters will now [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe decoded safely; entries that fail decoding will simply use the raw name, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmatching original fallback behavior.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes are made to tests or harness code, so existing CI and fuzzing flows[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain intact.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
